</div>

This field will not be present if message was blocked by AutoMod or content was not part of any message



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">alert_system_message_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The id of any system auto moderation messages posted as a result of this action

This field will not be present if this event does not correspond to an action with type &lbrace;@link AutoModerationActionType.SendAlertMessage &rbrace;

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">content</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The user generated text content

`MESSAGE_CONTENT` (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) gateway intent is required to receive non-empty values from this field



</div>

  <code className="text-sm">matched_keyword</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

</div>

  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The substring in content that triggered the rule

`MESSAGE_CONTENT` (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) gateway intent is required to receive non-empty values from this field



</div></div>

<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">data</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIChatInputApplicationCommandInteractionData | APIMessageApplicationCommandInteractionData | ... 9 more ... | (APIChatInputApplicationCommandInteractionData & Required<...>)"}</code>
</div>

The command data payload



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIPartialInteractionGuild"}</code>
</div>

The guild it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The guild it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">member</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIInteractionGuildMember"}</code>
</div>

Guild member data for the invoking user, including permissions

**This is only sent when an interaction is invoked in a guild**



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">user</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIUser"}</code>
</div>

User object for the invoking user, if invoked in a DM



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">token</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

A continuation token for responding to the interaction



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">version</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"1"}</code>
</div>

Read-only property, always `1`



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">message</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessage"}</code>
</div>

For components, the message they were attached to



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">app_permissions</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Bitwise set of permissions the app or bot has within the channel the interaction was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_locale</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"\"id\" | \"en-US\" | \"en-GB\" | \"bg\" | \"zh-CN\" | \"zh-TW\" | \"hr\" | \"cs\" | \"da\" | \"nl\" | \"fi\" | \"fr\" | \"de\" | \"el\" | \"hi\" | \"hu\" | \"it\" | \"ja\" | \"ko\" | \"lt\" | \"no\" | \"pl\" | \"pt-BR\" | \"ro\" | \"ru\" | ... 6 more ... | \"vi\""}</code>
</div>

The guild's preferred locale, if invoked in a guild



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">entitlements</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIEntitlement[]"}</code>
</div>

For monetized apps, any entitlements for the invoking user, representing access to premium SKUs



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">authorizing_integration_owners</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIAuthorizingIntegrationOwnersMap"}</code>
</div>

Mapping of installation contexts that the interaction was authorized for to related user or guild IDs.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">context</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"InteractionContextType"}</code>
</div>

Context where the interaction was triggered from



</div></div>

### GatewayMessageCreateDispatchData

https://discord.com/developers/docs/topics/gateway-events#message-create

</div>

Member properties for this message's author

The member object exists in `MESSAGE_CREATE` and `MESSAGE_UPDATE` events
from text-based guild channels

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/guild#guild-member-object

</div>

Users specifically mentioned in the message

The `member` field is only present in `MESSAGE_CREATE` and `MESSAGE_UPDATE` events
from text-based guild channels

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/user#user-object
See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/guild#guild-member-object



</div>

  <code className="text-sm">flags</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"MessageFlags"}</code>
</div>

Message flags combined as a bitfield

See https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bit_field



</div>

  <code className="text-sm">id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

ID of the message



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">application_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

If the message is a response to an Interaction, this is the id of the interaction's application



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">type</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"MessageType"}</code>

</div>

  <code className="text-sm">channel_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

ID of the channel the message was sent in



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">author</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIUser"}</code>
</div>

The author of this message (only a valid user in the case where the message is generated by a user or bot user)

If the message is generated by a webhook, the author object corresponds to the webhook's id,
username, and avatar. You can tell if a message is generated by a webhook by checking for the `webhook_id` property

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/user#user-object



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">content</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Contents of the message

The `MESSAGE_CONTENT` privileged gateway intent is required for verified applications to receive a non-empty value from this field

In the Discord Developers Portal, you need to enable the toggle of this intent of your application in **Bot &gt; Privileged Gateway Intents**.
You also need to specify the intent bit value (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) if you are connecting to the gateway

See https://support-dev.discord.com/hc/articles/4404772028055



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">

</div>

</div>

When this message was edited (or null if never)



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

</div>

Whether this was a TTS message



</div>

Whether this message mentions everyone



</div>

Roles specifically mentioned in this message

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">mention_channels</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIChannelMention[]"}</code>
</div>

Channels specifically mentioned in this message

Not all channel mentions in a message will appear in `mention_channels`.
- Only textual channels that are visible to everyone in a lurkable guild will ever be included
- Only crossposted messages (via Channel Following) currently include `mention_channels` at all

If no mentions in the message meet these requirements, this field will not be sent

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#channel-mention-object



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">attachments</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIAttachment[]"}</code>
</div>

Any attached files

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#attachment-object

The `MESSAGE_CONTENT` privileged gateway intent is required for verified applications to receive a non-empty value from this field

In the Discord Developers Portal, you need to enable the toggle of this intent of your application in **Bot &gt; Privileged Gateway Intents**.
You also need to specify the intent bit value (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) if you are connecting to the gateway

See https://support-dev.discord.com/hc/articles/4404772028055



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">embeds</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIEmbed[]"}</code>
</div>

Any embedded content

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#embed-object

The `MESSAGE_CONTENT` privileged gateway intent is required for verified applications to receive a non-empty value from this field

In the Discord Developers Portal, you need to enable the toggle of this intent of your application in **Bot &gt; Privileged Gateway Intents**.
You also need to specify the intent bit value (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) if you are connecting to the gateway

See https://support-dev.discord.com/hc/articles/4404772028055



</div>

  <code className="text-sm">reactions</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIReaction[]"}</code>
</div>

Reactions to the message

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#reaction-object



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">nonce</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string | number"}</code>
</div>

A nonce that can be used for optimistic message sending (up to 25 characters)

**You will not receive this from further fetches. This is received only once from a `MESSAGE_CREATE`
event to ensure it got sent**

</div>

If the message is generated by a webhook, this is the webhook's id



</div>

</div>

Sent with Rich Presence-related chat embeds

</div>

  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Partial<APIApplication>"}</code>
</div>

Sent with Rich Presence-related chat embeds

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/application#application-object



</div>

  <code className="text-sm">message_reference</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessageReference"}</code>
</div>

Reference data sent with crossposted messages, replies, pins, and thread starter messages

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#message-reference-object-message-reference-structure



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">referenced_message</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessage"}</code>
</div>

The message associated with the `message_reference`

This field is only returned for messages with a `type` of `19` (REPLY).

If the message is a reply but the `referenced_message` field is not present,
the backend did not attempt to fetch the message that was being replied to,
so its state is unknown.

If the field exists but is `null`, the referenced message was deleted

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#message-object



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">interaction_metadata</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessageInteractionMetadata"}</code>
</div>

Sent if the message is sent as a result of an interaction

- unstable:


</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">thread</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIThreadChannel"}</code>
</div>

Sent if a thread was started from this message



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">components</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIActionRowComponent<APIMessageActionRowComponent>[]"}</code>
</div>

Sent if the message contains components like buttons, action rows, or other interactive components

The `MESSAGE_CONTENT` privileged gateway intent is required for verified applications to receive a non-empty value from this field

In the Discord Developers Portal, you need to enable the toggle of this intent of your application in **Bot &gt; Privileged Gateway Intents**.
You also need to specify the intent bit value (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) if you are connecting to the gateway

See https://support-dev.discord.com/hc/articles/4404772028055



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">sticker_items</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIStickerItem[]"}</code>
</div>

Sent if the message contains stickers

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/sticker#sticker-item-object



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">position</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

A generally increasing integer (there may be gaps or duplicates) that represents the approximate position of the message in a thread

It can be used to estimate the relative position of the message in a thread in company with `total_message_sent` on parent thread



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">role_subscription_data</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessageRoleSubscriptionData"}</code>
</div>

Data of the role subscription purchase or renewal that prompted this `ROLE_SUBSCRIPTION_PURCHASE` message



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">resolved</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIInteractionDataResolved"}</code>
</div>

Data for users, members, channels, and roles in the message's auto-populated select menus

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/interactions/receiving-and-responding#interaction-object-resolved-data-structure



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">poll</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIPoll"}</code>
</div>

A poll!

The `MESSAGE_CONTENT` privileged gateway intent is required for verified applications to receive a non-empty value from this field

In the Discord Developers Portal, you need to enable the toggle of this intent of your application in **Bot &gt; Privileged Gateway Intents**.
You also need to specify the intent bit value (`1 &lt;&lt; 15`) if you are connecting to the gateway

See https://support-dev.discord.com/hc/articles/4404772028055



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">message_snapshots</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessageSnapshot[]"}</code>
</div>

The message associated with the message_reference. This is a minimal subset of fields in a message (e.g. author is excluded.)



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">call</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessageCall"}</code>

</div>

Channels specifically mentioned in this message

Not all channel mentions in a message will appear in `mention_channels`.
- Only textual channels that are visible to everyone in a lurkable guild will ever be included
- Only crossposted messages (via Channel Following) currently include `mention_channels` at all

If no mentions in the message meet these requirements, this field will not be sent

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#channel-mention-object

### GatewayThreadMemberUpdateDispatchData

</div>

Additional information about the user

**This field is omitted on the member sent within each thread in the `GUILD_CREATE` event**

**This field is only present when `with_member` is set to true when calling `List Thread Members` or `Get Thread Member`**

### GatewayThreadCreateDispatchData

  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

Number of messages (not including the initial message or deleted messages) in a thread

If the thread was created before July 1, 2022, it stops counting at 50 messages



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">member_count</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

The approximate member count of the thread, does not count above 50 even if there are more members



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">owner_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

ID of the thread creator



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">total_message_sent</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

Number of messages ever sent in a thread

Similar to `message_count` on message creation, but won't decrement when a message is deleted



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">applied_tags</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string[]"}</code>
</div>

The IDs of the set of tags that have been applied to a thread in a thread-only channel



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">flags</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"ChannelFlags"}</code>
</div>

No Description



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The id of the channel



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">type</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"ThreadChannelType"}</code>
</div>

The type of the channel

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#channel-object-channel-types



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">rate_limit_per_user</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

Amount of seconds a user has to wait before sending another message (0-21600);
bots, as well as users with the permission `MANAGE_MESSAGES` or `MANAGE_CHANNELS`, are unaffected

`rate_limit_per_user` also applies to thread creation. Users can send one message and create one thread during each `rate_limit_per_user` interval.

For thread channels, `rate_limit_per_user` is only returned if the field is set to a non-zero and non-null value.
The absence of this field in API calls and Gateway events should indicate that slowmode has been reset to the default value.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">last_message_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The id of the last message sent in this channel (may not point to an existing or valid message)



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">last_pin_timestamp</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

When the last pinned message was pinned.
This may be `null` in events such as `GUILD_CREATE` when a message is not pinned



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The id of the guild (may be missing for some channel objects received over gateway guild dispatches)



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">position</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

Sorting position of the channel



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">name</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The name of the channel (1-100 characters)



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">permission_overwrites</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIOverwrite[]"}</code>
</div>

Explicit permission overwrites for members and roles

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/channel#overwrite-object



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">nsfw</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"boolean"}</code>
</div>

Whether the channel is nsfw



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">parent_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

ID of the parent category for a channel (each parent category can contain up to 50 channels)

OR

ID of the parent channel for a thread



</div></div>

  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"boolean"}</code>
</div>

Used to specify if we want the presences of the matched members



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">nonce</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Nonce to identify the Guild Members Chunk response

Nonce can only be up to 32 bytes. If you send an invalid nonce it will be ignored and the reply member_chunk(s) will not have a `nonce` set.

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/topics/gateway-events#guild-members-chunk



</div></div>

### GatewayRequestGuildMembersDataWithQuery



<div className='*:border-b [&>*:last-child]:border-b-0'><div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">query</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

String that username starts with, or an empty string to return all members



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">limit</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

Maximum number of members to send matching the `query`;
a limit of `0` can be used with an empty string `query` to return all members



</div>

  <code className="text-sm">guild_id</code>
